April 15, 2003 Tuesday


HEADLINE: Late Night Political Humor.


BODY:

Jay Leno:

"Welcome to the Tonight Show. Nice to have you all here. I guess this is like Holy Week, isn't it? Well, it is. We had Palm Sunday. It's also Passover. This week is also Easter. You know, between the rescue of our POWs and the Tigers winning a game, this is truly the week of miracles, isn't it?"

Jay Leno:

"Boy, I had a good day today. Listen to this. I bought four chairs and a table on Ebay from some guy in Baghdad, 12 bucks, 12 bucks." 

Jay Leno:

"Today, President Bush announced that all this time he's been mispronouncing the word Iraq. He says it's actually pronounced 'Syria.'"

Jay Leno:

"Hey, this is getting scary now. And, you know, the press keeps asking President Bush, 'When is the war going to end? When will this war end?' See, I think this war will end officially the day after the 2004 elections. Because if President Bush learned anything from his father, it's don't end a war too soon."

Jay Leno:

"And the leaders of France, Russia and Germany, as I call them, our Axis of Envy, they've gathered for a summit on what their part, what their role will be in the rebuilding of Iraq. You know, I think France should participate in rebuilding Iraq, I do. I mean, think about it, when it comes to having experience about what do after losing a war, nobody does it better than them."

Jay Leno:

"Here's something that came as quite a shock, the Canadian prime minister has ordered the Canadian navy not to capture any of Saddam Hussein's henchmen if they try to flee Iraq by sea. Today at the Pentagon, they were stunned. They had no idea Canada had a navy."

Jay Leno:

"President Bush said this week, that Slovakia has already offered their help in de-mining Iraq. They want to help de-mine Iraq. And listen to this. Exxon Mobil has offered their help in de-oiling Iraq."

Jay Leno:

"Here's something a little frightening. CNN reports that when they broke into Uday Hussein's palace, you hear about this? They found pornography, Cuban cigars and pictures of President Bush's twin daughters. I'm sorry, that was Bill Clinton's bunker."

Jay Leno:

"I guess Marines found a bunch of these suicide vests placed neatly on hangers and covered in plastic. Did you hear about this? Army intelligence says they found them just in time, 'cause in another week the suicide jacket and pants would have been ready."

Jay Leno:

"See, that's why guys wear suicide vests. In a suicide vest, if something goes wrong, yeah, you still die. See, suicide pants, something goes wrong, you just wish you were dead.'

Jay Leno:

"Our commanders in the Gulf are warning that Iraq is still a very, very dangerous place. Not as dangerous as riding shotgun with Snoop Dogg, but still pretty dangerous."

Jay Leno:

"A number of people in the White House now are concerned that Michael Moore, you remember Michael - he said all that stuff at the Academy Awards -- there you go. Huge hand. Yeah. Well, they're worried that Michael Moore might be invited to the annual White House correspondents dinner in which President Bush will speak. They're not worried Moore will try to disrupt the evening, you know, they just don't want to get stuck behind him in the buffet line."

Jay Leno:

"Officials at the baseball Hall of Fame in Cooperstown, New York, have canceled the celebration of the 15th anniversary of the baseball movie 'Bull Durham,' you hear about this? Because Susan Sarandon and Tim Robbins have these anti-war, anti-Bush views. Canceled at the Hall of Fame. And even worse news for Pete Rose. Turns out, he bet on Iraq."

Jay Leno:

"Tim Robbins sent a letter saying he did not realize baseball was a Republican sport. You think it's Republican or Democratic? What do you think? Well, it's got a lot of multimillionaires, so it could be Republican. But then you got a lot of switch hitters who grab themselves, so it could be Democratic."

David Letterman:

"They've gone crazy over there in Iraq, they're just looting like crazy. It's unbelievable. I haven't seen so much merchandise flying out of stores since, well, Winona Ryder."

David Letterman:

"Yesterday in downtown Baghdad, they toppled the statue of Sean Penn."

David Letterman:

"I don't care what they say about weapons of mass destruction or not, but Iraq is just a horrible place. Just listen to what our troops he found over there -- torture chambers, nerve gas, all-male country clubs."

David Letterman:

"But the US military has vowed to get Saddam Hussein. In fact, they're going to do it tomorrow night when he goes out to mail his taxes."

David Letterman:

"And now, President Bush is saying Syria, Syria has weapons of mass destruction. Gee, I wonder where he's heading with this?"

April 16, 2003 Wednesday


HEADLINE: Late Night Political Humor.


BODY:

Jay Leno:

"Welcome to the Tonight Show. What a crowd! All right. Yeah! You sound like you all think you're getting refunds or something. Man!"

Jay Leno:

"Well, today was tax day. Of course, the one day when every American wishes he was an illegal alien." 

Jay Leno:

"Well, actually, technically, people talk about this. They debate this. But technically, you're not paying taxes. According to the Bush Administration, your bank account is being liberated."

Jay Leno:

"This is the day Americans have to deal with their two favorite government agencies -- the IRS and the Post Office. You know what I do to make it a full day? I just drop by the Department of Motor Vehicles."

Jay Leno:

"Anybody here afraid of being audited? Oh, people worry about this, but according to statistics, listen to this, you are five times more likely to get murdered, to get murdered, than face criminal prosecution for tax evasion. Isn't that amazing? Here's the ironic thing, if you did get murdered it would probably be by some criminal who doesn't pay taxes in the first place. He's got time to murder you because he's not home doing his taxes."

Jay Leno:

"Well, folks, with 90% of the bombs in, MSNBC now calling the war for the US. Looks like it's over."

Jay Leno:

"Let's see what's happening in Iraq. Or as the Pentagon calls it, gateway to Syria!"

Jay Leno:

"For the first time ever, the people of Iraq are united. Tell you what I'm talking about -- today on CNN I saw a Kurd, a Shiite and a member of the Republican Guard all working together to cart off a big-screen TV."

Jay Leno:

"Whoever's put in charge of rebuilding Iraq, here's what they should do. Put all the furniture into the rooms first, then make the doorways smaller than the average house. This way, next time the looters won't be able to get the stuff out."

Jay Leno:

"Well, did you hear about what they found in Uday's house? You know, Saddam Hussein's son? Did you hear about this? Besides indoor pools and his own zoo and tons of pornography, they also discovered Uday had his own brothel. He had a whorehouse built into his house. This is what happens when single guys decorate their own place. They go overboard!"

Jay Leno:

"You know, for the first weeks of the war, the ratings at the cable news networks were huge, huge, way, way up, but they've fallen the past couple of weeks. You know why? Most of their early viewers were Iraqi soldiers tuning in to find out from Geraldo where our Marines were."

Jay Leno:

"I guess you heard, last night another suicide driver was stopped and taken into custody. Rodney King! Rodney King! Back in the news again. Oh, good old Rodney."

Jay Leno:

"Now, here's something I don't understand. The Utah Supreme Court ruled this week an atheist has the right to pray at government- sponsored public functions. Who is the atheist praying to?"

Jay Leno:

"That shows you how screwed up our government is. The only people allowed to pray in public on government land are atheists."

Jay Leno:

"And as you know, Hillary Clinton has a new book coming out. They can't get the title. Hillary has this book, supposed to be due in August. And they keep coming up with different titles to see which ones the public likes -- I guess this is the latest one. Okay, this is by Hillary Clinton: "Honey, I'm sorry I'm not Fat Enough.' Okay, they probably won't go with that one then!"

David Letterman:

"Last night, what a nasty audience we had. Rough crowd. Right after the show, they toppled my statue."

David Letterman:

"They found one of Saddam Hussein's family palaces. ... The family palace, this is what the US troops found - a private zoo, Prozac, pictures of naked women. It was just like Michael Jackson's place, except for the naked women."

David Letterman:

"The troops did not find any nerve gas. However, they did find large drums of Aqua Velva."

David Letterman:

"They found tequila, Viagra, and Prozac. And coincidentally, that's how I got through the shingles."

David Letterman:

"The Iraqis need to be taught how to behave. For example, you can't just go out rioting and looting. You can't do that, you know. Unless your team wins a championship. Then everything is fine."

April 17, 2003 Thursday


HEADLINE: Late Night Political Humor.


BODY:

Jay Leno:

"According to the latest poll, just out today, 71% of the American people approve of President Bush. Well, Bush is very, very happy. Well, of course he's happy. It only took 49% of the vote to win the election."

Jay Leno:

"Well, now that the war in Iraq is over, a lot of people want President Bush to focus on the economy. You know who really wants Bush to focus on the economy? Syria. Yeah, Syria." 

Jay Leno:

"A lot of people are afraid they're going to go to war with Syria. Syria is not Iraq, okay? It is less dangerous. It's less of an enemy. It has less of an army. And it has less oil."

Jay Leno:

"American officials have accused Syria of possessing chemical weapons. And today, Hans Blix, the UN inspector, he offered to spend the next three months not finding any of their chemical weapons, too."

Jay Leno:

"The Iraqis sat down for talks on how to put together a postwar government. They would have sat down yesterday, but somebody stole all the couches."

Jay Leno:

"Now there are reports from Baghdad that officials are taking bribes for favors, they're giving jobs to their relatives, they're taking money under the table from contractors. Do you know what that means? This war is less than a week old, already they have an American-style democracy."

Jay Leno:

"And I guess you know all of Iraq's oil fields are now under US control, which is kind of ironic since all the gas stations here are run by Middle Easterners."

Jay Leno:

"French President Jacques Chirac called President Bush yesterday for the first time in two months in an attempt to try to warm relations. He wants to find a French role in the construction of Iraq. He wants something the French can do. See, now you know why France used to be called 'Gaul.'"

Jay Leno:

"And today the homeland security code was lowered. It was lowered, except here in Los Angeles, where it was raised to code red. Nothing to do with Middle East. Just Rodney King out driving again."

Jay Leno:

"Oh, here you go, Monica Lewinsky hosting a reality show for Fox beginning next week. You know about this show? Show's called 'Mr. Personality,' where a woman will try to choose between 20 men who all have masks on. And Monica Lewinsky will offer her dating advice. Well, who better to offer advice on choosing a guy without seeing his face than Monica Lewinsky?"

David Letterman:

"On my lunch hour, I'm walking through Central Park, and I saw a beautiful spring sight here in New York City. It was a robin, like one of the first robins of spring, building a nest out of duct tape."

David Letterman:

"We're learning more and more about Saddam Hussein and his family than we did before the war. And US troop have busted into many of the family palaces. Listen to what they found. They break into one of the family palaces, here's what they find. Tequila. Hell, I got tequila. Tequila. Viagra. And Prozac. Or as I call it, a pre-show cocktail."

David Letterman:

"You can tell that the war is nearly over. Tonight on ABC they have a two-hour special, Dick Clark's Rocking Downfall of Baghdad."

David Letterman:

"Even though Iraq has been liberated now, we have to teach them about democracy and the voting, the election process. Because there's still some confusion about democracy and the election process -- oh, no, wait a minute, that's Florida."

David Letterman:

"It's interesting, I was looking at my calendar and this year we have a late Passover. We also have a late Easter. And a late Saddam Hussein."

Jay Leno:

"Hey, how about this? President Bush went on TV to announce that from now on, every three weeks, we're gonna kick another country's ass. Yeah! Every three weeks, yeah."

"And more good news today -- Iraq announced they will stay open during the remodeling. So that's good news, too."

"And Pentagon officials said today that our military did not use the majority of the ammunition we brought to Iraq. We still have ammunition left over, which is not good news for Syria."

Jay Leno:

"In fact, if you don't know this, Syria is an ancient Arabic word for 'next.'"

Jay Leno:

"Today, US forces in Iraq captured one of Saddam's half-brothers. Barzan, I think that guy's name is. Barzan. These people sound like something from 'The Jungle Book.' Barzan."

Jay Leno:

"Anyway, I guess Barzan was one of Saddam's top military advisers. You can imagine how bad he would have gotten his ass kicked if he didn't have these advisers."

Jay Leno:

"You know what I noticed? How we never seem to go to war with countries you want to visit? No, we never liberate Aruba or Tahiti."

Jay Leno:

"US forces did a terrific job in capturing that terrorist mastermind, Abu Abbas. You remember the Achille Lauro hijacking? They killed that poor person, like 16 years ago. Now we have to decide what to do with him. I mean, the family of the man he killed, they want him sent here. The Italians want to extradite him to Italy. The Palestinians want him sent to Palestine. You know what would make everybody happy? Let's send a piece of him to each place."

Jay Leno:

"He was in Iraq. Sources say Abbas never made any attempt to hide himself. He lived a normal life. He was out in the open, in a country that protected him from the US. It's the same deal Roman Polanski has with France, basically. Oh, yeah. I'm way off base. Shut up."

Jay Leno:

"Under a new Bush Administration proposal, DNA profiles of people who have been arrested will be added to the FBI's database. And some of President Bush's advisers told him, 'That sounds like Big Brother.' Bush was furious. He told him, 'Hey, I don't have any big brothers -- I'm the oldest.'"

Jay Leno:

"And this week, in 1961, was the famous Bay of Pigs invasion. See, a lot of the young people today don't remember the Bay of Pigs. They think it's some bad reality show on Fox. 'If you loved the girls on "Temptation Island," you'll love 'Bay of Pigs.'"

Jay Leno:

"And another Saddam Hussein statue came tumbling down today. Rodney King hit it with his car."

Jay Leno:

"According to a poll in the LA Times, Governor Gray Davis is the least popular Governor in 55 years. And here's the sad part, they've only been doing this poll for 12 years."

Jay Leno:

"And the New York Post reporting that Bill Clinton is in Chappaqua, New York, writing his memoirs, and Hillary Clinton is in Washington writing hers. Which is amazing. Two people are getting paid millions of dollars to write memoirs about events they couldn't remember when they were under oath."

David Letterman:

"What's the matter, you folks couldn't get into Syria?"

David Letterman:

"We now know that Saddam Hussein's ex-wives are hiding out in Syria. His three ex-wives are hanging out in Syria. So that's one place we don't need to look for him."

David Letterman:

"Special Ops forces have rescued an American League umpire, last night in Chicago."

HEADLINE: Late Night Political Humor.


BODY:

"Let's say you stole the bear. You even get the bear back to your house. Now what do you do? 'Ahmed, put him in the spare bedroom, you idiot.'"

"American forces in Iraq found $650 million in cash, in cash, in bills. $650 million hidden in a sealed-up cottage. See, this is why Bush wants to invade Iraq. The entire country is like money and oil. It's like Republican Disneyland over there. Just cash and oil."

"This is like, what, the third half-brother? How many half-brothers? What, was Hussein's father in the NBA? How many kids does he have?"

"Well, more and more details coming out about Saddam Hussein, or as they call him now, Barney Rubble."

Jay Leno:

"And about his decadent lifestyle. Very decadent lifestyle. Apparently, every one of his palaces contains a huge collection of pornography, or as he called it, weapons of masturbation."

Boy, that is every 'C' student's dream come true, isn't it? Go back to your class reunion as the President."

Jay Leno:

"Starting this week, 44 commercial airline pilots have passed a law enforcement training course in Georgia that makes them eligible to carry handguns on flights. Two of the pilots didn't complete the course because they weren't able to pass the psychological exam. They couldn't pass the psychological exam. So all they're qualified to do now is fly a plane with people on it."

Jay Leno:

"Hey, let me tell you, this gun training class is pretty rigorous. In order to be certified they have to be able to shoot ten of those little tiny liquor bottles off of a fence in a row."

Jay Leno:

"According to the New York Post, Hillary Clinton is having problems. She's supposed to write that book. And she says the problem she's having with writing her memoirs is she doesn't want to write about Monica Lewinsky, Paula Jones or Jennifer Flowers. Well, of course she doesn't. Those are Bill's memoirs."

Jay Leno:

In this case, the guys' faces are hidden by a mask. See, in Monica's case, the guy's face was hidden by a desk. But it's a little different."

"But God bless Dennis Kucinich. He's doing terrible. He keeps running. In fact, his slogan is, 'Don't look back.' Of course, he doesn't have to look back. There's nobody behind him."

Jay Leno:

"Actually, political experts are saying the reason John Kerry's doing so well is because he is electable, that's the term they use. Electable. So is Al Gore, he even got elected and it didn't help him at all."

Jay Leno:

"And Howard Dean is fighting back. He said about his campaign shake- up -- you know, he replaced his campaign manager and other people -- Howard Dean said, 'From now on, you will see a leaner, meaner organization.' Meaner? How scary -- what, is he going to be biting people now?"

Jay Leno:

"Wesley Clark -- anybody for him? You know, this guy's interesting because he had spoken now both in favor and against the decision to go to war in Iraq. In fact, this weekend in South Carolina, he's going to be debating himself."

Jay Leno:

"This has been a tough week for President Bush. Yesterday, the former US chief weapons inspector, David Kay, testified before Congress about the weapons of mass destruction. Did you hear about this? He said, 'We were almost all wrong.' You never hear a politician say that. He said, 'We were almost all wrong.' President Bush hadn't heard those words since he took his SATs."

Jay Leno:

"Let me tell you something. There might not have been any weapons of mass destruction in Iraq, but you gotta give President Bush credit for one thing he was right about. Turns out there are rocks on Mars."

Jay Leno:

"And the winter storms continue to batter New York City. Man, it was cold back East. But I thought this was nice. Today, Martha Stewart gave each and every one of the jurors a $40,000 mink coat."

Jay Leno:

"I tell you, Martha Stewart's lawyer didn't win any points with the jury today when he said, 'Martha is a person who is just like you, if you were perfect.'"

Jay Leno:

"One of Martha's attorneys called the government's case against her today guesswork. That's what he called it, guesswork. Unlike Martha's stock trading, which had no guesswork at all. That was based on solid insider information."

"Last night, there was another Democratic presidential debate. How many watched it? Nobody? In fact, the first question the moderator asked Dennis Kucinich, he said, 'What are you doing here? Can't you take a hint? It's over!'"

Jay Leno:

"I don't want to say Dennis Kucinich is doing badly, but last night, his campaign was featured on the CBS show 'Without A Trace."

Jay Leno:

"It's starting to get nasty. Last night during the debates, John Edwards said, 'A President must be able to walk and chew gum at the same time.' I don't know. Shouldn't the qualifications be a little tougher than that? Aren't we lowering the bar just a little too much?"

Jay Leno:

"Actually, today, President Bush responded. He said, 'Chewing gum and walking's not hard. Chewing a pretzel -- oh, that's tricky."

Jay Leno:

"It's so stupid how petty these things get. A number of plastic surgeons are claiming that looking at John Kerry now as opposed to a few months ago -- they believe he's had botox shots. They claim a number of his worry lines have vanished. They haven't vanished. Just Howard Dean is wearing them now."

Jay Leno:

"And Howard Dean announced this week that his staff is leaner and meaner. Leaner, because he's letting some of them go, and meaner, because he's not paying them anymore."

Jay Leno:

"Dean announced he's pulling his TV ads off this week, pulling them off, pulling them off, and he's asked his staff to skip paychecks for the next couple of weeks because they're out of money. See, this way, he can keep the campaign going to explain to the American people how he's the best guy to balance the budget."

Jay Leno:

"And earlier this week, Vice President Dick Cheney met with the Pope at the Vatican. Did you see him on the news? He got down on his knees, clutched his heart, and then keeled over. I don't know what happened."

Jay Leno:

"You know, today is Vice President Dick Cheney's birthday. He's 63. But in heart attack years, that's 190, I believe.

Jay Leno:

"And they had a pretty wild party. I understand a registered nurse jumped out of a giant bran muffin. What a party. Huge, huge party."

Jay Leno:

"Now, listen. If you're thinking of getting the Vice President a gift, you can't do wrong with signing your organ donor card."

HEADLINE: Late Night Political Humor


BODY:

Jay Leno:

"What a crowd. You sound like Bill Clinton after watching the lingerie bowl. Yeah!'

Jay Leno:

"Wasn't it a great game? Boston Red Sox and the Panthers both played a great game. Did I say Red Sox? It's Monday. I was at a party. The Patriots and the Panthers. You know why I did that? Because I lost 1,000 bucks. I bet that Janet Jackson would show her left breast." 

Jay Leno:

"Did you watch that halftime show? Man. Finally, a halftime show for straight guys."

Jay Leno:

"You know the whole deal. Janet was doing a duet with Justin Timberlake, and at the end, he ripped off part of her costume, exposing one of her breasts, which is kind of ironic. For once, a Jackson getting molested. Has that ever happened?"

Jay Leno:

"And Justin Timberlake, God bless him, I love when they get handlers and lawyers and PR people. What did he call this? A 'wardrobe malfunction.' That's what he said. That's what he called it. A 'wardrobe malfunction.' What was the malfunction? What, were both breasts supposed to pop out?"

Jay Leno:

"And today, CBS, they apologized for Janet showing her breast. Forget that. How about CBS apologizing for Richard showing his fat ass on 'Survivor?'"

Jay Leno:

"I love how high and mighty they get. CBS said that moment did not conform to CBS broadcast standards. What standards? They showed a commercial with a horse farting in a woman's face. Where are these standards?"

Jay Leno:

"What standards? People act like they're so shocked at seeing a breast in the halftime show. Do you watch the Super Bowl? Every commercial was for some kind of impotency drug. They finally show something that might give you a real erection, and, oh, my God, what are we going to do?"

Jay Leno:

"Today the chairman of the FCC announced he is launching an immediate and swift investigation into what they're calling 'Nipplegate.' That's what this is. Nipplegate."

Jay Leno:

"Nipplegate. Immediate and swift investigation. However, we still have to wait until next year to find out why we went to war with Iraq. But we'll find out what happened with her breast probably in 48 hours."

Jay Leno:

"Today is Groundhog Day. Happy Groundhog Day, everybody. This year, President Bush saw his shadow, and it was John Kerry. Hey, what are the odds of that?'

Jay Leno:

"As you know, on Groundhog Day, the old-timers, they feel they can predict whether we'll have an early spring or six more weeks of winter by whether or not the groundhog sees his shadow, or, as President Bush calls that, 'reliable intelligence.'"

Jay Leno:

"A spokesman for the military said today they expect to capture Osama bin Laden later this year. I understand they're shooting for the first week in November."

Jay Leno:

"And President Bush said today he now wants to know the facts. He wants to know the facts about Iraq's weapons. You know, before we do something stupid like go to war."

Jay Leno:

"You know what's interesting, during his testimony last week before the Senate Armed Services Committee, former US chief weapons inspector David Kay, he defended President Bush for saying Iraq had weapons of mass destruction. Kay blamed the intelligence community. And then he said, and I quote, he doesn't want anyone 'confusing President Bush with the intelligence community.'"

Jay Leno:

"And the state of Wisconsin says it will now give people a $10,000 tax donation for donating an organ. You can knock $10,000 off your taxes if you donate an organ. How creepy is that? You're filling out a joint return with the wife. 'Honey, how many kidneys you got? Put me down for 20 grand.'"

David Letterman:

"Of course, all the excitement during half time, the game is interrupted when this naked guy runs onto the field. And he's got like a Website address all over his body, printed on the back side of him and I'm thinking 'Wow, that Howard Dean is really desperate.'"

David Letterman:

"How many of you saw that thing with Janet Jackson? I'll be honest, I was happy to see that happen, that Janet Jackson thing, because that meant for one night I wasn't the biggest boob on CBS."

David Letterman:

"And I guess the guy, what's his name, Justin Timberlake? Yeah, he's saying that the problem was a ward robe malfunction. I was thinking, 'Gees, the last time I was involved in a wardrobe malfunction, I became a father!'"

David Letterman:

"Then of course, after the game, President Bush calls the winning team, he calls the Patriots. And listen to this, former President Clinton called Janet Jackson. It's crazy!"
